TITLE      Neutron cross sections for nucleosynthesis studies     V010200100003 
AUTHOR     (Z.Y.Bao, H.Beer, F.Kaeppeler, F.Voss, K.Wisshak,      V010200100004 
            T.Rauscher)                                           V010200100005 
INSTITUTE  (2GERKFK,2SWTBAS)                                      V010200100006 
REFERENCE  (J,AND,76,70,2000) Update of 1987 and 1992 evaluation  V010200100007 
           (S,EUR-23883,55,2010) I.Dillmann+, KADoNiS v0.3        V010200100008 
           (J,AJ/S,80,403,1992)  H.Beer+, previous compilation    V010200100009 
           (J,AND,36,411,1987)   Z.Y.Bao+, previous compilation   V010200100010 
METHOD     Evaluation:                                            V010200100011 
           - The experimental results for nuclei between H and Bi V010200100012 
             were critically surveyed, renormalized to selected   V010200100013 
             standard cross sections.                             V010200100014 
           - Cross sections calculated by statistical model NON-  V010200100015 
             SMOKER were adopted in those cases where             V010200100016 
             experimental information is still missing (majority  V010200100017 
             of radioactive nuclei defining the s-process         V010200100018 
             branching).                                          V010200100019 
COMMENT    KADoNiS v0.3 was released in 28 August 2009.           V010200100020 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) Essentially evaluated from the systematic   V010200100021 
            errors quoted for the experimental data.              V010200100022 
           Since most publications were not detailed enough with  V010200100023 
            respect to error estimates, no critical judgment on   V010200100024 
            these was attempted.                                  V010200100025 
           Nevertheless, these error estimates appeared fairly    V010200100026 
            realistic in general.                                 V010200100027

           (20131127U) On. REFERENCE revised, REL-REF deleted     V010200100029
